Gremlins 2: The New Batch! Whether you're all about Mohawk's menacing chaos or Gizmo's battle-ready
transformation, these articulated, 3.75" scale figures will let you recreate all the action-packed moments from the

blistered cardback-perfect for display if you'd like to keep them mint. If you've ever wondered what it's like to
have your very own Mogwai showdown, now's your chance!

Gizmo is all geared up for action! The new 3.75" scale, articulated battle-ready Gizmo ReAction Figure, inspired
by the 1990 film Gremlins 2: The New Batch, brings the movie's hero to life like never before. With film-accurate
details, Gizmo is ready to defend himself-and your collection-with his pencil and paperclip bow and arrow
accessory! Packaged on a full color blistered cardback, this figure is the perfect addition to any Gremlins fan's
shelf. Collect yours today!

- Inspired by the 1990 film Gremlins 2: The New Batch

cardback
